<a id="23872" class="Symbol">...</a> <a id="23876" class="Symbol">|</a> <a id="23878" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Relation.Nullary.html#641" class="InductiveConstructor">yes</a> <a id="23882" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#209" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟨</a> <a id="23884" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Inference.md %}{% raw %}#23884" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="23886" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Inference.md %}{% raw %}#11827" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⇒</a> <a id="23888" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Inference.md %}{% raw %}#23888" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="23890" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#209" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="23892" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Inference.md %}{% raw %}#23892" class="Bound">⊢L</a> <a id="23895" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#209" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟩</a> <a id="23897" class="Keyword">with</a> <a id="23902" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Inference.md %}{% raw %}#23383" class="Function">inherit</a> <a id="23910" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="23912" class="Bound">M</a> <a id="23914" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Inference.md %}{% raw %}#23884" class="Bound">A</a>
<a id="23916" class="Symbol">...</a>    <a id="23923" class="Symbol">|</a> <a id="23925" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Relation.Nullary.html#668" class="InductiveConstructor">no</a>  <a id="23929" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Inference.md %}{% raw %}#23929" class="Bound">¬⊢M</a>          <a id="23942" class="Symbol">=</a>  <a id="23945" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Relation.Nullary.html#668" class="InductiveConstructor">no</a>  <a id="23949" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="23950" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Inference.md %}{% raw %}#21192" class="Function">¬arg</a> <a id="23955" class="Bound">⊢L</a> <a id="23958" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Inference.md %}{% raw %}#23929" class="Bound">¬⊢M</a><a id="23961" class="Symbol">)</a>
<a id="23963" class="Symbol">...</a>    <a id="23970" class="Symbol">|</a> <a id="23972" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Relation.Nullary.html#641" class="InductiveConstructor">yes</a> <a id="23976" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Inference.md %}{% raw %}#23976" class="Bound">⊢M</a>           <a id="23989" class="Symbol">=</a>  <a id="23992" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Relation.Nullary.html#641" class="InductiveConstructor">yes</a> <a id="23996" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#209" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟨</a> <a id="23998" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="24000" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#209" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="24002" class="Bound">⊢L</a> <a id="24005" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Inference.md %}{% raw %}#14569" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">·</a> <a id="24007" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Inference.md %}{% raw %}#23976" class="Bound">⊢M</a> <a id="24010" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#209" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟩</a>
<a id="24012" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Inference.md %}{% raw %}#23285" class="Function">synthesize</a> <a id="24023" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Inference.md %}{% raw %}#24023" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="24025" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="24026" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Inference.md %}{% raw %}#24026" class="Bound">M</a> <a id="24028" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Inference.md %}{% raw %}#12297" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">↓</a> <a id="24030" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Inference.md %}{% raw %}#24030" class="Bound">A</a><a id="24031" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="24033" class="Keyword">with</a> <a id="24038" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Inference.md %}{% raw %}#23383" class="Function">inherit</a> <a id="24046" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Inference.md %}{% raw %}#24023" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="24048" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Inference.md %}{% raw %}#24026" class="Bound">M</a> <a id="24050" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Inference.md %}{% raw %}#24030" class="Bound">A</a>
<a id="24052" class="Symbol">...</a> <a id="24056" class="Symbol">|</a> <a id="24058" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Relation.Nullary.html#668" class="InductiveConstructor">no</a>  <a id="24062" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Inference.md %}{% raw %}#24062" class="Bound">¬⊢M</a>             <a id="24078" class="Symbol">=</a>  <a id="24081" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Relation.Nullary.html#668" class="InductiveConstructor">no</a>  <a id="24085" class="Symbol">(λ{</a> <a id="24089" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#209" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟨</a> <a id="24091" class="Symbol">_</a> <a id="24093" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#209" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="24095" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Inference.md %}{% raw %}#14668" class="InductiveConstructor">⊢↓</a> <a id="24098" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Inference.md %}{% raw %}#24098" class="Bound">⊢M</a> <a id="24101" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#209" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟩</a>  <a id="24104" class="Symbol">→</a>  <a id="24107" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Inference.md %}{% raw %}#24062" class="Bound">¬⊢M</a> <a id="24111" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Inference.md %}{% raw %}#24098" class="Bound">⊢M</a> <a id="24114" class="Symbol">})</a>
<a id="24117" class="Symbol">...</a> <a id="24121" class="Symbol">|</a> <a id="24123" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Relation.Nullary.html#641" class="InductiveConstructor">yes</a> <a id="24127" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Inference.md %}{% raw %}#24127" class="Bound">⊢M</a>              <a id="24143" class="Symbol">=</a>  <a id="24146" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Relation.Nullary.html#641" class="InductiveConstructor">yes</a> <a id="24150" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#209" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟨</a> <a id="24152" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="24154" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#209" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="24156" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Inference.md %}{% raw %}#14668" class="InductiveConstructor">⊢↓</a> <a id="24159" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Inference.md %}{% raw %}#24127" class="Bound">⊢M</a> <a id="24162" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#209" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟩</a>
</pre>{% endraw %}There are three cases:

* If the term is a variable `` ` x ``, we use lookup as defined above:

  + If it fails, then `¬∃` is evidence that there is no `A` such
    that `Γ ∋ x ⦂ A` holds.  Evidence that `` Γ ⊢ ` x ↑ A `` holds must
    have the form `` ⊢` ∋x ``, where `∋x` is evidence that `Γ ∋ x ⦂ A`,
    which yields a contradiction.

  + If it succeeds, then `∋x` is evidence that `Γ ∋ x ⦂ A`, and
    hence `` ⊢′ ∋x `` is evidence that `` Γ ⊢ ` x ↑ A ``.

* If the term is an application `L · M`, we recurse on the function `L`:

  + If it fails, then `¬∃` is evidence that there is no type such
    that `Γ ⊢ L ↑ _` holds.  Evidence that `Γ ⊢ L · M ↑ _` holds
    must have the form `⊢L · _`, where `⊢L` is evidence that
    `Γ ⊢ L ↑ _`, which yields a contradiction.

  + If it succeeds, there are two possibilities:

    - One is that `⊢L` is evidence that `` Γ ⊢ L ⦂ `ℕ ``.  Evidence
      that `Γ ⊢ L · M ↑ _` holds must have the form `⊢L′ · _` where
      `⊢L′` is evidence that `Γ ⊢ L ↑ A ⇒ B` for some types `A` and
      `B`.  Applying `uniq-↑` to `⊢L` and `⊢L′` yields a
      contradiction, since `` `ℕ `` cannot equal `A ⇒ B`.

    - The other is that `⊢L` is evidence that `Γ ⊢ L ↑ A ⇒ B`, in
      which case we recurse on the argument `M`:

      * If it fails, then `¬⊢M` is evidence that `Γ ⊢ M ↓ A` does
        not hold.  By `¬arg` applied to `⊢L` and `¬⊢M`, it follows
        that `Γ ⊢ L · M ↑ B` cannot hold.

      * If it succeeds, then `⊢M` is evidence that `Γ ⊢ M ↓ A`,
        and `⊢L · ⊢M` provides evidence that `Γ ⊢ L · M ↑ B`.

* If the term is a switch `M ↓ A` from synthesised to inherited,
  we recurse on the subterm `M`, supplying type `A` by inheritance:

  + If it fails, then `¬⊢M` is evidence that `Γ ⊢ M ↓ A` does not
    hold.  Evidence that `Γ ⊢ (M ↓ A) ↑ A` holds must have the
    form `⊢↓ ⊢M` where `⊢M` is evidence that `Γ ⊢ M ↓ A` holds,
    which yields a contradiction.

  + If it succeeds, then `⊢M` is evidence that `Γ ⊢ M ↓ A`,
    and `⊢↓ ⊢M` provides evidence that `Γ ⊢ (M ↓ A) ↑ A`.

We next consider the code for inheritance:

<a id="26303" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Inference.md %}{% raw %}#23383" class="Function">inherit</a> <a id="26311" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link <a id="27111" class="Symbol">...</a>       <a id="27121" class="Symbol">|</a> <a id="27123" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Relation.Nullary.html#668" class="InductiveConstructor">no</a> <a id="27126" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Inference.md %}{% raw %}#27126" class="Bound">¬⊢N</a>          <a id="27139" class="Symbol">=</a>  <a id="27142" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Relation.Nullary.html#668" class="InductiveConstructor">no</a>  <a id="27146" class="Symbol">(λ{</a> <a id="27150" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="27151" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Inference.md %}{% raw %}#15000" class="InductiveConstructor">⊢case</a> <a id="27157" class="Symbol">_</a> <a id="27159" class="Symbol">_</a> <a id="27161" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Inference.md %}{% raw %}#27161" class="Bound">⊢N</a><a id="27163" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="27165" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="27167" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Inference.md %}{% raw %}#27126" class="Bound">¬⊢N</a> <a id="27171" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Inference.md %}{% raw %}#27161" class="Bound">⊢N</a> <a id="27174" class="Symbol">})</a>

<a id="27488" class="Symbol">...</a> <a id="27492" class="Symbol">|</a> <a id="27494" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Relation.Nullary.html#641" class="InductiveConstructor">yes</a> <a id="27498" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#209" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟨</a> <a id="27500" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Inference.md %}{% raw %}#27500" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="27502" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#209" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="27504" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Inference.md %}{% raw %}#27504" class="Bound">⊢M</a> <a id="27507" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#209" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟩</a> <a id="27509" class="Keyword">with</a> <a id="27514" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Inference.md %}{% raw %}#27500" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="27516" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Inference.md %}{% raw %}#16815" class="Function Operator">≟Tp</a> <a id="27520" class="Bound">B</a>
<a id="27522" class="Symbol">...</a>   <a id="27528" class="Symbol">|</a> <a id="27530" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Relation.Nullary.html#668" class="InductiveConstructor">no</a>  <a id="27534" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Inference.md %}{% raw %}#27534" class="Bound">A≢B</a>             <a id="27550" class="Symbol">=</a>  <a id="27553" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Relation.Nullary.html#668" class="InductiveConstructor">no</a>  <a id="27557" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="27558" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Inference.md %}{% raw %}#22103" class="Function">¬switch</a> <a id="27566" class="Bound">⊢M</a> <a id="27569" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Inference.md %}{% raw %}#27534" class="Bound">A≢B</a><a id="27572" class="Symbol">)</a>
<a id="27574" class="Symbol">...</a>   <a id="27580" class="Symbol">|</a> <a id="27582" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Relation.Nullary.html#641" class="InductiveConstructor">yes</a> <a id="27586" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Inference.md %}{% raw %}#27586" class="Bound">A≡B</a>             <a id="27602" class="Symbol">=</a>  <a id="27605" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Relation.Nullary.html#641" class="InductiveConstructor">yes</a> <a id="27609" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="27610" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Inference.md %}{% raw %}#15263" class="InductiveConstructor">⊢↑</a> <a id="27613" class="Bound">⊢M</a> <a id="27616" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Inference.md %}{% raw %}#27586" class="Bound">A≡B</a><a id="27619" class="Symbol">)</a>
</pre>{% endraw %}We consider only the cases for abstraction and
and for switching from inherited to synthesized:

* If the term is an abstraction `ƛ x ⇒ N` and the inherited type
  is `` `ℕ ``, then it is trivial that `` Γ ⊢ (ƛ x ⇒ N) ↓ `ℕ ``
  cannot hold.

* If the term is an abstraction `ƛ x ⇒ N` and the inherited type
  is `A ⇒ B`, then we recurse with context `Γ , x ⦂ A` on subterm
  `N` inheriting type `B`:

  + If it fails, then `¬⊢N` is evidence that `Γ , x ⦂ A ⊢ N ↓ B`
    does not hold.  Evidence that `Γ ⊢ (ƛ x ⇒ N) ↓ A ⇒ B` holds
    must have the form `⊢ƛ ⊢N` where `⊢N` is evidence that
    `Γ , x ⦂ A ⊢ N ↓ B`, which yields a contradiction.

  + If it succeeds, then `⊢N` is evidence that `Γ , x ⦂ A ⊢ N ↓ B`
    holds, and `⊢ƛ ⊢N` provides evidence that `Γ ⊢ (ƛ x ⇒ N) ↓ A ⇒ B`.

* If the term is a switch `M ↑` from inherited to synthesised,
  we recurse on the subterm `M`:

  + If it fails, then `¬∃` is evidence there is no `A` such
    that `Γ ⊢ M ↑ A` holds.  Evidence that `Γ ⊢ (M ↑) ↓ B` holds
    must have the form `⊢↑ ⊢M _` where `⊢M` is evidence that
    `Γ ⊢ M ↑ _`, which yields a contradiction.

  + If it succeeds, then `⊢M` is evidence that `Γ ⊢ M ↑ A` holds.
    We apply `_≟Tp_` do decide whether `A` and `B` are equal:

    - If it fails, then `A≢B` is evidence that `A ≢ B`.
      By `¬switch` applied to `⊢M` and `A≢B` it follow that
      `Γ ⊢ (M ↑) ↓ B` cannot hold.

    - If it succeeds, then `A≡B` is evidence that `A ≡ B`,
      and `⊢↑ ⊢M A≡B` provides evidence that `Γ ⊢ (M ↑) ↓ B`.

The remaining cases are similar, and their code can pretty much be
read directly from the corresponding typing rules.

## Testing the example terms

First, we copy a function introduced earlier that makes it easy to
compute the evidence that two variable names are distinct:
{% raw %}<pre class="Agda"><a id="_≠_"></a><a id="29422" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Inference.md %}{% raw %}#29422" class="Function Operator">_≠_</a> <a id="29426" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="29428" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="29430" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="29431" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Inference.md %}{% raw %}#29431" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="29433" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Inference.md %}{% raw %}#29433" class="Bound">y</a> <a id="29435" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="29437" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Inference.md %}{% raw %}#11766" class="Function">Id</a><a id="29439" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="29441" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="29443" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Inference.md %}{% raw %}#29431" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="29445" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality.Core.html#799" class="Function Operator">≢</a> <a id="29447" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Inference.md %}{% raw %}#29433" class="Bound">y</a>
<a id="29449" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Inference.md %}{% raw %}#29449" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="29451" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Inference.md %}{% raw %}#29422" class="Function Operator">≠</a> <a id="29453" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Inference.md %}{% raw %}#29453" class="Bound">y</a>  <a id="29456" class="Keyword">with</a> <a id="29461" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Inference.md %}{% raw %}#29449" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="29463" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Data.String.Properties.html#2569" class="Function Operator">≟</a> <a id="29465" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Inference.md %}{% raw %}#29453" class="Bound">y</a>
<a id="29467" class="Symbol">...</a>       <a id="29477" class="Symbol">|</a> <a id="29479" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Relation.Nullary.html#668" class="InductiveConstructor">no</a>  <a id="29483" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Inference.md %}{% raw %}#29483" class="Bound">x≢y</a>  <a id="29488" class="Symbol">=</a>  <a id="29491" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Inference.md %}{% raw %}#29483" class="Bound">x≢y</a>
<a id="29495" class="Symbol">...</a>       <a id="29505" class="Symbol">|</a> <a id="29507" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Relation.Nullary.html#641" class="InductiveConstructor">yes</a> <a id="29511" class="Symbol">_</a>    <a id="29516" class="Symbol">=</a>  <a id="29519" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Data.Empty.html#294" class="Function">⊥-elim</a> <a id="29526" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Inference.md %}{% raw %}#29555" class="Postulate">impossible</a>
  <a id="29539" class="Keyword">where</a> <a id="29545" class="Keyword">postulate</a> <a id="29555" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Inference.md %}{% raw %}#29555" class="Postulate">impossible</a> <a id="29566" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="29568" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Data.Empty.html#279" class="Datatype">⊥</a>
</pre>{% endraw %}
Here is the result of typing two plus two on naturals:

</pre>{% endraw %}We confirm that synthesis on the relevant term returns
natural as the type and the above derivation:
{% raw %}<pre class="Agda"><a id="30112" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Inference.md %}{% raw %}#30112" class="Function">_</a> <a id="30114" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="30116" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Inference.md %}{% raw %}#23285" class="Function">synthesize</a> <a id="30127" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Inference.md %}{% raw %}#11882" class="InductiveConstructor">∅</a> <a id="30129" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Inference.md %}{% raw %}#13252" class="Function">2+2</a> <a id="30133" href="Agda.Builtin.Equality.html#125" class="Datatype Operator">≡</a> <a id="30135" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Relation.Nullary.html#641" class="InductiveConstructor">yes</a> <a id="30139" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#209" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟨</a> <a id="30141" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Inference.md %}{% raw %}#11812" class="InductiveConstructor">`ℕ</a> <a id="30144" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#209" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="30146" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Inference.md %}{% raw %}#29634" class="Function">⊢2+2</a> <a id="30151" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#209" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟩</a>
<a id="30153" class="Symbol">_</a> <a id="30155" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="30157" href="Agda.Builtin.Equality.html#182" class="InductiveConstructor">refl</a>
</pre>{% endraw %}Indeed, the above derivation was computed by evaluating the term on
the left, with minor editing of the result.  The only editing required
was to replace Agda's representation of the evidence that two strings
are unequal (which it cannot print nor read) by equivalent calls to
`_≠_`.

</pre>{% endraw %}We confirm that synthesis on the relevant term returns
natural as the type and the above derivation:
{% raw %}<pre class="Agda"><a id="31299" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Inference.md %}{% raw %}#31299" class="Function">_</a> <a id="31301" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="31303" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Inference.md %}{% raw %}#23285" class="Function">synthesize</a> <a id="31314" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Inference.md %}{% raw %}#11882" class="InductiveConstructor">∅</a> <a id="31316" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Inference.md %}{% raw %}#13769" class="Function">2+2ᶜ</a> <a id="31321" href="Agda.Builtin.Equality.html#125" class="Datatype Operator">≡</a> <a id="31323" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Relation.Nullary.html#641" class="InductiveConstructor">yes</a> <a id="31327" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#209" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟨</a> <a id="31329" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Inference.md %}{% raw %}#11812" class="InductiveConstructor">`ℕ</a> <a id="31332" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#209" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="31334" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Inference.md %}{% raw %}#30519" class="Function">⊢2+2ᶜ</a> <a id="31340" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#209" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟩</a>
<a id="31342" class="Symbol">_</a> <a id="31344" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="31346" href="Agda.Builtin.Equality.html#182" class="InductiveConstructor">refl</a>
</pre>{% endraw %}Again, the above derivation was computed by evaluating the
term on the left and editing.

## Testing the error cases

It is important not just to check that code works as intended,
but also that it fails as intended.  Here are checks for
several possible errors:

Unbound variable:
{% raw %}<pre class="Agda"><a id="31641" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Inference.md %}{% raw %}#31641" class="Function">_</a> <a id="31643" class="Symbol">:</a> <a ## Erasure

From the evidence that a decorated term has the correct type it is
easy to extract the corresponding intrinsically-typed term.  We use the
name `DB` to refer to the code in
Chapter [DeBruijn]({{ site.baseurl }}/DeBruijn/).
It is easy to define an _erasure_ function that takes an extrinsic
type judgment into the corresponding intrinsically-typed term.

First, we give code to erase a type:
{% raw %}<pre class="Agda"><a id="∥_∥Tp"></a><a id="33200" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Inference.md %}{% raw %}#33200" class="Function Operator">∥_∥Tp</a> <a id="33206" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="33208" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Inference.md %}{% raw %}#11793" class="Datatype">Type</a> <a id="33213" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="33215" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/More.md %}{% raw %}#14469" class="Datatype">DB.Type</a>
<a id="33223" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Inference.md %}{% raw %}#33200" class="Function Operator">∥</a> <a id="33225" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Inference.md %}{% raw %}#11812" class="InductiveConstructor">`ℕ</a> <a id="33228" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Inference.md %}{% raw %}#33200" class="Function Operator">∥Tp</a>             <a id="33244" class="Symbol">=</a>  <a id="33247" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/More.md %}{% raw %}#14488" class="InductiveConstructor">DB.`ℕ</a>
<a id="33253" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Inference.md %}{% raw %}#33200" class="Function Operator">∥</a> <a id="33255" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Inference.md %}{% raw %}#33255" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="33257" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Inference.md %}{% raw %}#11827" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⇒</a> <a id="33259" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Inference.md %}{% raw %}#33259" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="33261" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Inference.md %}{% raw %}#33200" class="Function Operator">∥Tp</a>          <a id="33274" class="Symbol">=</a>  <a id="33277" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Inference.md %}{% raw %}#33200" class="Function Operator">∥</a> <a id="33279" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Inference.md %}{% raw %}#33255" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="33281" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Inference.md %}{% raw %}#33200" class="Function Operator">∥Tp</a> <a id="33285" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/More.md %}{% raw %}#14503" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">DB.⇒</a> <a id="33290" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Inference.md %}{% raw %}#33200" class="Function Operator">∥</a> <a id="33292" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Inference.md %}{% raw %}#33259" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="33294" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Inference.md %}{% raw %}#33200" class="Function Operator">∥Tp</a>
</pre>{% endraw %}It simply renames to the corresponding constructors in module `DB`.

Next, we give the code to erase a context:
{% raw %}<pre class="Agda"><a id="∥_∥Cx"></a><a id="33418" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Inference.md %}{% raw %}#33418" class="Function Operator">∥_∥Cx</a> <a id="33424" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="33426" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Inference.md %}{% raw %}#11860" class="Datatype">Context</a> <a id="33434" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="33436" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/More.md %}{% raw %}#14602" class="Datatype">DB.Context</a>

Next, we give the code to erase a lookup judgment:
{% raw %}<pre class="Agda"><a id="∥_∥∋"></a><a id="33617" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Inference.md %}{% raw %}#33617" class="Function Operator">∥_∥∋</a> <a id="33622" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="33646" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="33648" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Inference.md %}{% raw %}#33418" class="Function Operator">∥</a> <a </pre>{% endraw %}It simply drops the evidence that variable names are distinct.

Finally, we give the code to erase a typing judgment.
Just as there are two mutually recursive typing judgments,
there are two mutually recursive erasure functions:

</pre>{% endraw %}Erasure replaces constructors for each typing judgment
by the corresponding term constructor from `DB`.  The
constructors that correspond to switching from synthesized
to inherited or vice versa are dropped.

We confirm that the erasure of the type derivations in
this chapter yield the corresponding intrinsically-typed terms
from the earlier chapter:

## Bidirectional inference in Agda

Agda itself uses bidirectional inference.  This explains why
constructors can be overloaded while other defined names cannot ---
here by _overloaded_ we mean that the same name can be used for
constructors of different types.  Constructors are typed by
inheritance, and so the name is available when resolving the
constructor, whereas variables are typed by synthesis, and so each
variable must have a unique type.

Most top-level definitions in Agda are of functions, which are typed
by inheritance, which is why Agda requires a type declaration for
those definitions.  A definition with a right-hand side that is a term
typed by synthesis, such as an application, does not require a type
declaration.
{% raw %}<pre class="Agda"><a id="answer"></a><a id="36670" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Inference.md %}{% raw %}#36670" class="Function">answer</a> <a id="36677" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="36679" class="Number">6</a> <a id="36681" href="Agda.Builtin.Nat.html#501" class="Primitive Operator">*</a> <a id="36683" class="Number">7</a>
</pre>{% endraw %}

This chapter uses the following unicode:

    ↑  U+2191:  UPWARDS ARROW (\u)
    ∥  U+2225:  PARALLEL TO (\||)
